          <section class="album-reviews">
           <header class="album-reviews__header">
            <h1 class="album-reviews__heading">
             <a class="album-reviews__link" href="/reviews/albums/">
              Reviews
             </a>
            </h1>
           </header>
           <div class="album-review-hero hp-primary">
            <a aria-label="artwork" class="artwork" href="/reviews/albums/anita-baker-rapture/">
             <div class="">
              <img alt="Anita Baker: Rapture" class="album-review-hero__img" src="https://media.pitchfork.com/photos/605243f102674855a6d5be11/1:1/w_320/Anita%20Baker:%20Rapture.jpeg"/>
             </div>
            </a>
            <div class="album-details">
             <a class="album-link" href="/reviews/albums/anita-baker-rapture/">
              <ul class="artist-list">
               <li>
                Anita Baker
               </li>
              </ul>
              <h2 class="title">
               Rapture
              </h2>
             </a>
             <div class="meta">
              <div class="byline">
               <ul class="authors">
                <li>
                 <a class="linked display-name display-name--linked" href="/staff/brad-nelson/">
                  <span class="by">
                   by:
                  </span>
                  Brad Nelson
                 </a>
                </li>
               </ul>
               <ul class="genre-list genre-list--inline">
                <li class="genre-list__item">
                 <a class="genre-list__link" href="/reviews/albums/?genre=pop">
                  Pop/R&amp;B
                 </a>
                </li>
               </ul>
              </div>
             </div>
             <div class="abstract">
              <p>
               Each Sunday, Pitchfork takes an in-depth look at a significant album from the past, and any record not in our archives is eligible. Today we revisit Anita Baker’s timeless 1986 album, a slow-burning and symphonic piece of quiet storm R&amp;B that floods every sense.
              </p>
             </div>
            </div>
           </div>
           <div class="hp-reviews-secondary">
            <div class="album-review-hero album-review-hero--level-2">
             <a aria-label="artwork" class="artwork multi" href="/reviews/albums/bobby-womack-the-poet-the-poet-ii/">
              <div class="">
               <div class="lazy-image album-review-hero__img album-review-hero__img--multi" style="padding-bottom:calc(100% - 2px)">
               </div>
              </div>
             </a>
             <div class="album-details">
              <a class="album-link" href="/reviews/albums/bobby-womack-the-poet-the-poet-ii/">
               <ul class="artist-list">
                <li>
                 Bobby Womack
                </li>
               </ul>
               <h2 class="title">
                The Poet / The Poet II
               </h2>
              </a>
              <div class="meta">
               <div class="byline">
                <ul class="authors">
                 <li>
                  <a class="linked display-name display-name--linked" href="/staff/tarisai-ngangura/">
                   <span class="by">
                    by:
                   </span>
                   Tarisai Ngangura
                  </a>
                 </li>
                </ul>
                <ul class="genre-list genre-list--inline">
                 <li class="genre-list__item">
                  <a class="genre-list__link" href="/reviews/albums/?genre=jazz">
                   Jazz
                  </a>
                 </li>
                 <li class="genre-list__item">
                  <a class="genre-list__link" href="/reviews/albums/?genre=rock">
                   Rock
                  </a>
                 </li>
                </ul>
               </div>
              </div>
              <div class="abstract">
               <p>
                This latest reissue from the legendary soul singer features some of the greatest love songs ever made. It also reminds us of a tall and tarnished legacy left behind.
               </p>
              </div>
             </div>
            </div>
            <div class="album-review-hero album-review-hero--level-2">
             <a aria-label="artwork" class="artwork" href="/reviews/albums/lana-del-rey-chemtrails-over-the-country-club/">
              <div class="">
               <div class="lazy-image album-review-hero__img" style="padding-bottom:calc(100% - 2px)">
               </div>
              </div>
             </a>
             <div class="album-details">
              <a class="album-link" href="/reviews/albums/lana-del-rey-chemtrails-over-the-country-club/">
               <ul class="artist-list">
                <li>
                 Lana Del Rey
                </li>
               </ul>
               <h2 class="title">
                Chemtrails Over the Country Club
               </h2>
              </a>
              <div class="meta">
               <div class="byline">
                <ul class="authors">
                 <li>
                  <a class="linked display-name display-name--linked" href="/staff/mina-tavakoli/">
                   <span class="by">
                    by:
                   </span>
                   Mina Tavakoli
                  </a>
                 </li>
                </ul>
                <ul class="genre-list genre-list--inline">
                 <li class="genre-list__item">
                  <a class="genre-list__link" href="/reviews/albums/?genre=pop">
                   Pop/R&amp;B
                  </a>
                 </li>
                </ul>
               </div>
              </div>
              <div class="abstract">
               <p>
                Lana Del Rey’s sixth album dials back the grandiosity in favor of smaller, more intimate moments. It carries a roaming spirit of folk and Americana without losing the romantic melodrama of her best work.
               </p>
              </div>
             </div>
            </div>
            <div class="album-review-hero album-review-hero--level-2">
             <a aria-label="artwork" class="artwork" href="/reviews/albums/benny-the-butcher-harry-fraud-the-plugs-i-met-2/">
              <div class="">
               <div class="lazy-image album-review-hero__img" style="padding-bottom:calc(100% - 2px)">
               </div>
              </div>
             </a>
             <div class="album-details">
              <a class="album-link" href="/reviews/albums/benny-the-butcher-harry-fraud-the-plugs-i-met-2/">
               <ul class="artist-list">
                <li>
                 Benny the Butcher
                </li>
                <li>
                 Harry Fraud
                </li>
               </ul>
               <h2 class="title">
                The Plugs I Met 2
               </h2>
              </a>
              <div class="meta">
               <div class="byline">
                <ul class="authors">
                 <li>
                  <a class="linked display-name display-name--linked" href="/staff/pete-tosiello/">
                   <span class="by">
                    by:
                   </span>
                   Pete Tosiello
                  </a>
                 </li>
                </ul>
                <ul class="genre-list genre-list--inline">
                 <li class="genre-list__item">
                  <a class="genre-list__link" href="/reviews/albums/?genre=rap">
                   Rap
                  </a>
                 </li>
                </ul>
               </div>
              </div>
              <div class="abstract">
               <p>
                On his latest nine-track triumph, the Griselda star finds an easy chemistry with Harry Fraud, whose syrupy samples lend poignancy to these stories of hustling and survivor’s remorse.
               </p>
              </div>
             </div>

             All Album Reviews
            </a>

            <div class="hp-feature-hero features">
             <a class="artwork" href="/features/rising/cassandra-jenkins-an-overview-on-phenomenal-nature-interview/">
              <span class="sr-only">
               Cassandra Jenkins’ Hypnotic Folk Music Turns Everyday Moments Into Monuments
              </span>
              <div class="lazy-image" style="padding-bottom:50%">
              </div>
             </a>
             <div class="feature-details">
              <a class="title" href="/features/rising/cassandra-jenkins-an-overview-on-phenomenal-nature-interview/">
               <h2>
                Cassandra Jenkins’ Hypnotic Folk Music Turns Everyday Moments Into Monuments
               </h2>
              </a>
              <div class="cat-date">
               <div class="type-category">
                <a href="/features/">
                 Features
                </a>
                <span class="splitter">
                 /
                </span>
                <a class="category" href="/features/rising/">
                 Rising
                </a>
               </div>
               <ul class="authors">
                <li>
                 <span class="display-name">
                  by:
                  <!-- -->
                  Vrinda Jagota
                 </span>
                </li>
               </ul>
              </div>
              <div class="abstract-container">
               <div class="abstract">
                <p>
                 In this Rising interview, the New York singer-songwriter talks about making art out of interactions with strangers and how her experiences with the late indie legend David Berman inspired her brilliant new album.
                </p>
               </div>
              </div>
             </div>
            </div>
           </div>

           <div class="hp-feature-hero features">
            <a class="artwork" href="/features/article/the-endless-life-cycle-of-japanese-city-pop/">
             <span class="sr-only">
              The Endless Life Cycle of Japanese City Pop
             </span>
             <div class="lazy-image" style="padding-bottom:50%">
             </div>
            </a>
            <div class="feature-details">
             <a class="title" href="/features/article/the-endless-life-cycle-of-japanese-city-pop/">
              <h2>
               The Endless Life Cycle of Japanese City Pop
              </h2>
             </a>
             <div class="cat-date">
              <div class="type-category">
               <a href="/features/">
                Features
               </a>
               <span class="splitter">
                /
               </span>
               <a class="category" href="/features/article/">
                Longform
               </a>
              </div>
              <ul class="authors">
               <li>
                <span class="display-name">
                 by:
                 <!-- -->
                 Cat Zhang
                </span>
               </li>
              </ul>
             </div>
             <div class="abstract-container">
              <div class="abstract">
               <p>
                Boosted by the YouTube recommendations algorithm, and now TikTok memes, an American-influenced strain of vintage Japanese music has become a perennial cult hit online. The trend says more about Western perceptions of the East than the other way around.
               </p>
              </div>
             </div>
            </div>
           </div>
           <div class="hp-feature-hero video">
            <a class="artwork" href="/tv/57-from-our-partners/driven-by-sound-part-ii-featuring-madlib-and-kaytranada/">
             <span class="sr-only">
              Driven by Sound: Part II | Featuring Madlib &amp; Kaytranada
             </span>
             <div class="lazy-image" style="padding-bottom:50%">
             </div>
            </a>
            <div class="feature-details">
             <a class="title" href="/tv/57-from-our-partners/driven-by-sound-part-ii-featuring-madlib-and-kaytranada/">
              <h2>
               Driven by Sound: Part II | Featuring Madlib &amp; Kaytranada
              </h2>
             </a>
             <div class="cat-date">
              <div class="type-category">
               <a href="/tv/">
                Video
               </a>
               <span class="splitter">
                /
               </span>
               <a class="category" href="/tv/57-from-our-partners/">
                From Our Partners
               </a>
              </div>
              <ul class="authors">
               <li>
                <span class="display-name">
                 by:
                 <!-- -->
                 Pitchfork
                </span>
               </li>
              </ul>
             </div>
             <div class="abstract-container">
              <div class="abstract">
               <p>
                In the second episode of a two-part documentary, producers Madlib and Kaytranada learn more about the installation of the custom in-dash record player in the Lexus IS Wax. Madlib then takes the Lexus IS Wax Edition for a spin to premiere his and Kaytranada’s exclusive double-sided single. Produced by Pitchfork with Lexus.
               </p>
              </div>

         <div class="image-bg">
          <img alt=""/>
         </div>
         <div class="container-fluid">
          <div class="row">
           <a href="/features/lists-and-guides/">
            <h1 class="page-title list-section-title">
             <span>
              Lists &amp; Guides
             </span>
            </h1>
           </a>
           <div class="lists">
            <ul class="list-column">
             <li>
              <span class="year">
               2020
              </span>
              <a data-bg="//cdn.pitchfork.com/static/images/Lists_ModuleBg_2012Albums.png" href="/topics/the-best-music-of-2020/">
               Year in Music
              </a>

        <section class="more-recent-reviews">
         <h1 class="page-title">
          <span>
           More Recent Reviews
          </span>
         </h1>
         <div class="container-fluid">
          <div class="row">
           <div class="album-review-hero album-review-hero--level-3">
            <a aria-label="artwork" class="artwork" href="/reviews/albums/chad-vangaalen-worlds-most-stressed-out-gardener/">
             <div class="">
              <div class="lazy-image album-review-hero__img" style="padding-bottom:calc(100% - 2px)">
              </div>
             </div>
            </a>
            <div class="album-details">
             <a class="album-link" href="/reviews/albums/chad-vangaalen-worlds-most-stressed-out-gardener/">
              <ul class="artist-list">
               <li>
                Chad VanGaalen
               </li>
              </ul>
              <h2 class="title">
               World’s Most Stressed Out Gardener
              </h2>
             </a>
             <div class="meta">
              <div class="byline">
               <ul class="authors">
                <li>
                 <a class="linked display-name display-name--linked" href="/staff/zach-schonfeld/">
                  <span class="by">
                   by:
                  </span>
                  Zach Schonfeld
                 </a>
                </li>
               </ul>
              </div>
              <ul class="genre-list genre-list--inline">
               <li class="genre-list__item">
                <a class="genre-list__link" href="/reviews/albums/?genre=rock">
                 Rock
                </a>
               </li>
              </ul>
             </div>
             <div class="abstract">
              <p>
               Holed up in his DIY inventor’s laboratory,  VanGaalen delivers his most abrasive, unstable collection in years. Even this notorious Canadian recluse can't stop a little apocalyptic dread from creeping in.
              </p>
             </div>
            </div>
           </div>
           <div class="album-review-hero album-review-hero--level-3">
            <a aria-label="artwork" class="artwork" href="/reviews/albums/guapdad-4000-llmind-1176/">
             <div class="">
              <div class="lazy-image album-review-hero__img" style="padding-bottom:calc(100% - 2px)">
              </div>
             </div>
            </a>
            <div class="album-details">
             <a class="album-link" href="/reviews/albums/guapdad-4000-llmind-1176/">
              <ul class="artist-list">
               <li>
                Guapdad 4000
               </li>
               <li>
                !llmind
               </li>
              </ul>
              <h2 class="title">
               1176
              </h2>
             </a>
             <div class="meta">
              <div class="byline">
               <ul class="authors">
                <li>
                 <a class="linked display-name display-name--linked" href="/staff/stephen-kearse/">
                  <span class="by">
                   by:
                  </span>
                  Stephen Kearse
                 </a>
                </li>
               </ul>
              </div>
              <ul class="genre-list genre-list--inline">
               <li class="genre-list__item">
                <a class="genre-list__link" href="/reviews/albums/?genre=rap">
                 Rap
                </a>
               </li>
              </ul>
             </div>
             <div class="abstract">
              <p>
               The Oakland rapper known for his standout scam records sinks into a more reflective mood on his latest LP. The cost of this pensive turn is a loss of personality.
              </p>
             </div>
            </div>
           </div>
           <div class="album-review-hero album-review-hero--level-3">
            <a aria-label="artwork" class="artwork" href="/reviews/albums/leanne-betasamosake-simpson-theory-of-ice/">
             <div class="">
              <div class="lazy-image album-review-hero__img" style="padding-bottom:calc(100% - 2px)">
              </div>
             </div>
            </a>
            <div class="album-details">
             <a class="album-link" href="/reviews/albums/leanne-betasamosake-simpson-theory-of-ice/">
              <ul class="artist-list">
               <li>
                Leanne Betasamosake Simpson
               </li>
              </ul>
              <h2 class="title">
               Theory of Ice
              </h2>
             </a>
             <div class="meta">
              <div class="byline">
               <ul class="authors">
                <li>
                 <a class="linked display-name display-name--linked" href="/staff/grayson-currin/">
                  <span class="by">
                   by:
                  </span>
                  Grayson Haver Currin
                 </a>
                </li>
               </ul>
              </div>
              <ul class="genre-list genre-list--inline">
               <li class="genre-list__item">
                <a class="genre-list__link" href="/reviews/albums/?genre=folk">
                 Folk/Country
                </a>
               </li>
              </ul>
             </div>
             <div class="abstract">
              <p>
               On an album with the musical charms of British art-rock, the Indigenous writer and scholar uses our connections with water to explore the revolutionary power of community.
              </p>
             </div>
            </div>
           </div>
           <div class="album-review-hero album-review-hero--level-3">
            <a aria-label="artwork" class="artwork" href="/reviews/albums/thirdface-do-it-with-a-smile/">
             <div class="">
              <div class="lazy-image album-review-hero__img" style="padding-bottom:calc(100% - 2px)">
              </div>
             </div>
            </a>
            <div class="album-details">
             <a class="album-link" href="/reviews/albums/thirdface-do-it-with-a-smile/">
              <ul class="artist-list">
               <li>
                Thirdface
               </li>
              </ul>
              <h2 class="title">
               Do It With a Smile
              </h2>
             </a>
             <div class="meta">
              <div class="byline">
               <ul class="authors">
                <li>
                 <a class="linked display-name display-name--linked" href="/staff/nina-corcoran/">
                  <span class="by">
                   by:
                  </span>
                  Nina Corcoran
                 </a>
                </li>
               </ul>
              </div>
              <ul class="genre-list genre-list--inline">
               <li class="genre-list__item">
                <a class="genre-list__link" href="/reviews/albums/?genre=metal">
                 Metal
                </a>
               </li>
              </ul>
             </div>
             <div class="abstract">
              <p>
               The Nashville-based hardcore punk band’s exhilarating debut is a call-to-arms that could inspire even the most acquiescent to take action.
              </p>
             </div>
            </div>
           </div>

   (function userSegments(doc) {
  
  const pageLocation = encodeURIComponent(window.location.href);
  function addScript(src) {
    var s = document.createElement('script');
    s.src = src;
    s.async = true;
    document.body.appendChild(s);
  }
  addScript('/user-context?referrer=' + encodeURIComponent(document.referrer) + '&verso=false' + (typeof paymentForm !== 'undefined' ? '&paymentForm=' + paymentForm : '') + '&location=' + pageLocation);

   (function insertInterlude(brand, domain) {
    var src = 'https://' + domain + '/interlude/' + brand + '.js';
